The subsequent `kickstart -k` would start a new process before port 18789 was released, leaving two competing gateway processes. The TUI then sees a flood of `run error: terminated` errors because `KeepAlive=true` keeps trying to restart the failing new process.\\n\\nReal-world trigger: manually running `launchctl unload + load` (e.g. to apply a plist edit) bypasses OpenClaw&#39;s wait logic entirely — the old process keeps the port, the new one fails, and launchd loops.\\n\\n## Root cause\\n\\n```\\nwaitForPidExit(pid)  ← polls process.kill(pid, 0) up to 10s\\n  if timeout → returns void   ← 🐛 old process may still hold the port\\n                                  next kickstart -k races with it\\n```\\n\\n## Fix\\n\\nTwo new helpers:\\n\\n| Helper | What it does |\\n|--------|-------------|\\n| `waitForPidExit(pid)` | Same poll loop, now returns `boolean` (true = gone) |\\n| `ensurePidGone(pid)` | Waits for graceful exit → SIGKILL fallback → polls 3s for kill to land |\\n\\n`restartLaunchAgent()` and `stopLaunchAgent()` both use `ensurePidGone()` so **the port is guaranteed free before the new process is started** and **`openclaw gateway stop` returns only after the process is truly dead**.\\n\\n## Sequence after fix\\n\\n```\\nbootout (SIGTERM)\\n  └─ ensurePidGone(previousPid)\\n       ├─ wait up to 10s for graceful exit  → done ✓\\n       └─ (if still alive) SIGKILL + wait 3s → done ✓\\nbootstrap + kickstart -k   ← port guaranteed free\\n```\\n\\n## Tests\\n\\n21 existing `launchd.test.ts` tests pass unchanged.\"\n    state: closed\n    draft: false\n    merged: false\n    html_url: \"https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/43961\"\n    user:\n      login: happydog-intj\n      id: 212984\n      profile_url: \"https://github.com/happydog-intj\"\n      avatar_url: \"https://avatars.githubusercontent.com/u/212984?v=4\"\n    labels[2]: gateway,\"size: XL\"\n    head:\n      ref: fix/gateway-restart-race\n      sha: fc8a9fe5ecf0aebaba455ee9e57d2469ab63bf46\n      repo:\n        full_name: happydog-intj/openclaw\n        description: \"Your own personal AI assistant. The subsequent `kickstart -k` would start a new process before port 18789 was released, leaving two competing gateway processes. The TUI then sees a flood of `run error: terminated` errors because `KeepAlive=true` keeps trying to restart the failing new process.\\n\\nReal-world trigger: manually running `launchctl unload + load` (e.g. to apply a plist edit) bypasses OpenClaw&#39;s wait logic entirely — the old process keeps the port, the new one fails, and launchd loops.\\n\\n## Root cause\\n\\n```\\nwaitForPidExit(pid)  ← polls process.kill(pid, 0) up to 10s\\n  if timeout → returns void   ← 🐛 old process may still hold the port\\n                                  next kickstart -k races with it\\n```\\n\\n## Fix\\n\\nTwo new helpers:\\n\\n| Helper | What it does |\\n|--------|-------------|\\n| `waitForPidExit(pid)` | Same poll loop, now returns `boolean` (true = gone) |\\n| `ensurePidGone(pid)` | Waits for graceful exit → SIGKILL fallback → polls 3s for kill to land |\\n\\n`restartLaunchAgent()` and `stopLaunchAgent()` both use `ensurePidGone()` so **the port is guaranteed free before the new process is started** and **`openclaw gateway stop` returns only after the process is truly dead**.\\n\\n## Sequence after fix\\n\\n```\\nbootout (SIGTERM)\\n  └─ ensurePidGone(previousPid)\\n       ├─ wait up to 10s for graceful exit  → done ✓\\n       └─ (if still alive) SIGKILL + wait 3s → done ✓\\nbootstrap + kickstart -k   ← port guaranteed free\\n```\\n\\n## Tests\\n\\n21 existing `launchd.test.ts` tests pass unchanged.\"\n   179→    state: closed\n   180→    draft: false\n   181→    merged: false\n   182→    html_url: \"https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/43961\"\n The subsequent `kickstart -k` would start a new process before port 18789 was released, leaving two competing gateway processes. The TUI then sees a flood of `run error: terminated` errors because `KeepAlive=true` keeps trying to restart the failing new process.\\n\\nReal-world trigger: manually running `launchctl unload + load` (e.g. to apply a plist edit) bypasses OpenClaw&#39;s wait logic entirely — the old process keeps the port, the new one fails, and launchd loops.\\n\\n## Root cause\\n\\n```\\nwaitForPidExit(pid)  ← polls process.kill(pid, 0) up to 10s\\n  if timeout → returns void   ← 🐛 old process may still hold the port\\n                                  next kickstart -k races with it\\n```\\n\\n## Fix\\n\\nTwo new helpers:\\n\\n| Helper | What it does |\\n|--------|-------------|\\n| `waitForPidExit(pid)` | Same poll loop, now returns `boolean` (true = gone) |\\n| `ensurePidGone(pid)` | Waits for graceful exit → SIGKILL fallback → polls 3s for kill to land |\\n\\n`restartLaunchAgent()` and `stopLaunchAgent()` both use `ensurePidGone()` so **the port is guaranteed free before the new process is started** and **`openclaw gateway stop` returns only after the process is truly dead**.\\n\\n## Sequence after fix\\n\\n```\\nbootout (SIGTERM)\\n  └─ ensurePidGone(previousPid)\\n       ├─ wait up to 10s for graceful exit  → done ✓\\n       └─ (if still alive) SIGKILL + wait 3s → done ✓\\nbootstrap + kickstart -k   ← port guaranteed free\\n```\\n\\n## Tests\\n\\n21 existing `launchd.test.ts` tests pass unchanged.\"\n    state: closed\n    draft: false\n    merged: false\n    html_url: \"https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/43961\"\n    user:\n      login: happydog-intj\n      id: 212984\n      profile_url: \"https://github.com/happydog-intj\"\n      avatar_url: \"https://avatars.githubusercontent.com/u/212984?v=4\"\n    labels[2]: gateway,\"size: XL\"\n    head:\n      ref: fix/gateway-restart-race\n      sha: fc8a9fe5ecf0aebaba455ee9e57d2469ab63bf46\n      repo:\n        full_name: happydog-intj/openclaw\n        description: \"Your own personal AI assistant. Only `openclaw gateway install` works, which is wrong for a normal stop/start cycle.\\n\\n## Root cause\\n\\n`src/cli/daemon-cli/lifecycle-core.ts:208-217` — `runServiceStart()` calls `handleServiceNotLoaded()` when `isLoaded` returns false. This only prints hints, never calls `service.restart()`.\\n\\nMeanwhile, `service.restart()` (`restartLaunchAgent` at `launchd.ts:593-603`) already handles the &#34;not loaded&#34; case by calling `bootstrapLaunchAgentOrThrow` to re-register and start the service.\\n\\n## User impact\\n\\n`gateway stop` → `gateway start` is broken on macOS. Every macOS user who stops the gateway must run `gateway install` to recover. Breaks expected service lifecycle.\\n\\n## Fix\\n\\nWhen service is not loaded, attempt `service.restart()` first (which handles re-bootstrapping on all platforms). {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01MBA3VP8JQDWNz34HeM2Ddm","type":"tool_result","content":"total_count: 3787\nincomplete_results: false\nitems[10]:\n  - id: 4131207416\n    number: 54058\n    state: closed\n    locked: false\n    title: \"fix(feishu): default requireMention to false when groupPolicy is open\"\n    body: \"## Problem\\n\\nCloses #52553\\n\\nGroups with `groupPolicy: open` are expected to respond to all messages — the intent of \\\"open\\\" is that the bot participates in the conversation without restrictions. However, `requireMention` defaulted to `true` regardless of `groupPolicy`, causing **image, file, audio, and other non-text messages to be silently dropped** because they cannot carry `@`-mentions.\\n\\nThe drop path is the `requireMention && !ctx.mentionedBot` check in `handleFeishuMessage`. For open groups this is counterintuitive: a user who sets `groupPolicy: open` and sends an image gets no response, while a user who adds `requireMention: false` to their config gets the expected behaviour — but that extra step is not documented and easy to miss.\\n\\n## Fix\\n\\nWhen the effective `groupPolicy` is `\\\"open\\\"` and `requireMention` has not been explicitly configured at either the global or per-group level, resolve `requireMention` to `false` instead of `true`.\\n\\n**Changes:**\\n- `extensions/feishu/src/config-schema.ts` — remove `.default(true)` from the global `requireMention` field so that absent values stay `undefined` (enabling the conditional default below).\\n- `extensions/feishu/src/policy.ts` — `resolveFeishuReplyPolicy` accepts an optional `groupPolicy` parameter; when it is `\\\"open\\\"` the fallback default is `false` rather than `true`.\\n- `extensions/feishu/src/bot.ts` — pass the already-resolved `groupPolicy` into `resolveFeishuReplyPolicy`.\\n\\nUsers who want mention-required behaviour in open groups can still set `requireMention: true` explicitly — that value is respected as before.\\n\\n## Tests\\n\\nThree new regression tests in `bot.test.ts`:\\n1.
